Step 1 â€” Fix the Tailwind CSS pipeline (most likely culprit: wrong CSS file is being used)

Viteâ€™s default React template uses src/main.jsx and imports ./index.css.

Letâ€™s confirm itâ€™s correct and overwrite the file cleanly.

Step 2 â€” Fix your missing ./components/ui import

Right now your wireframe file expects:

â€¦but in jt-preview/src/ you donâ€™t have that.

You have two options:

Option B (guaranteed compile): Create a minimal src/components/ui.jsx file

If your original components folder doesnâ€™t actually contain the needed ui module, we can stub it so the app runs immediately.

Create this:

cat > src/components/ui.jsx <<'EOF'
import React from "react";

export function TopBar({ title = "Regenesis" }) {
  return (
    <div style={{ padding: "12px 16px", borderBottom: "1px solid #ddd", display: "flex", justifyContent: "space-between" }}>
      <div style={{ fontWeight: 700 }}>{title}</div>
      <div style={{ opacity: 0.7 }}>Wireframe</div>
    </div>
  );
}

export function LeftRail({ items = [], active, onSelect }) {
  return (
    <div style={{ width: 240, borderRight: "1px solid #ddd", padding: 12 }}>
      <div style={{ fontSize: 12, opacity: 0.6, marginBottom: 8 }}>Navigation</div>
      {items.map((it) => (
        <button
          key={it.key}
          onClick={() => onSelect?.(it.key)}
          style={{
            width: "100%",
            textAlign: "left",
            padding: "10px 12px",
            marginBottom: 8,
            borderRadius: 10,
            border: "1px solid #e5e5e5",
            background: it.key === active ? "#f2f2f2" : "white",
            cursor: "pointer",
          }}
        >
          {it.label}
        </button>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
}

export function PlaceholderPage({ title = "Coming soon", children }) {
  return (
    <div style={{ padding: 24 }}>
      <h2 style={{ margin: 0, marginBottom: 8 }}>{title}</h2>
      <div style={{ opacity: 0.8 }}>{children || "Placeholder content"}</div>
    </div>
  );
}
EOF


Then you must make sure your import matches that file:

In your wireframe file, change:

./components/ui â†’ ./components/ui.jsx

But Vite usually resolves .jsx automatically, so it should work as-is.

cat > src/components/ui.jsx <<'EOF'
import React from "react";

/**
 * Utility: classnames helper (very small substitute for clsx/cn patterns)
 */
export function cn(...vals) {
  return vals.filter(Boolean).join(" ");
}

/**
 * Basic UI atoms used by pages
 */
export function Badge({ children, className = "" }) {
  return (
    <span
      className={cn(
        "inline-flex items-center rounded-full border px-2 py-0.5 text-xs font-medium",
        className
      )}
    >
      {children}
    </span>
  );
}

export function Card({ title, children, className = "" }) {
  return (
    <div className={cn("rounded-xl border bg-white p-4 shadow-sm", className)}>
      {title ? <div className="mb-2 text-sm font-semibold">{title}</div> : null}
      {children}
    </div>
  );
}

export function PageHeader({ title, subtitle, right }) {
  return (
    <div className="mb-4 flex items-start justify-between gap-4">
      <div>
        <h1 className="text-xl font-semibold leading-tight">{title}</h1>
        {subtitle ? <p className="mt-1 text-sm opacity-70">{subtitle}</p> : null}
      </div>
      {right ? <div className="shrink-0">{right}</div> : null}
    </div>
  );
}

/**
 * App shell pieces referenced by JTCoachingAppShellWireframe.jsx
 */
export function TopBar({ title = "Regenesis" }) {
  return (
    <div className="flex items-center justify-between border-b bg-white px-4 py-3">
      <div className="font-semibold">{title}</div>
      <div className="text-sm opacity-60">Wireframe</div>
    </div>
  );
}

export function LeftRail({ items = [], active, onSelect }) {
  return (
    <div className="w-60 border-r bg-white p-3">
      <div className="mb-2 text-xs font-medium uppercase tracking-wide opacity-60">
        Navigation
      </div>

      <div className="flex flex-col gap-2">
        {items.map((it) => (
          <button
            key={it.key}
            onClick={() => onSelect?.(it.key)}
            className={cn(
              "rounded-xl border px-3 py-2 text-left text-sm transition",
              it.key === active ? "bg-gray-100" : "bg-white hover:bg-gray-50"
            )}
          >
            {it.label}
          </button>
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

export function PlaceholderPage({ title = "Coming soon", children }) {
  return (
    <div className="p-6">
      <h2 className="mb-2 text-lg font-semibold">{title}</h2>
      <div className="text-sm opacity-80">
        {children || "Placeholder content"}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
EOF

/**
 * Utility: classnames helper (very small substitute for clsx/cn patterns)

export function cn(...vals) {
  return vals.filter(Boolean).join(" ");
}

/**
 * Basic UI atoms used by pages
 */

  return (

      {children}
    </span>

}

}

Yep â€” I read it all. Two separate things are breaking you, and one of them is the real â€œwhy nothing rendersâ€.

Whatâ€™s actually happening (from your log)
A) Your src/components/ui.jsx keeps getting corrupted mid-write

Your terminal shows the cat > src/components/ui.jsx <<'EOF' ... EOF command, but then your paste cuts off before the EOF, and you start typing other commands (rm -rf ..., npm run dev, etc.) inside the file write.

Thatâ€™s why your file literally contains garbage like:

leading-tig<p className=...

uppercase tracking-wide opac

later: flex items-start justify-between Name="text-xl ...

When the file is malformed, esbuild says â€œNo matching exportâ€ because it canâ€™t parse the module correctly.

B) You also had a Tailwind/PostCSS error earlier

[postcss] Unexpected token, expected ";" (17:6) in src/index.css

That can also blank the page, but right now your bigger problem is the corrupted ui.jsx + missing import path.

The fix: do it in a way that cannot get corrupted

Instead of a giant paste, weâ€™ll delete the broken file and create a tiny, safe UI module first, confirm it compiles, then expand.

0) Stop Vite

Press Ctrl + C in the terminal where Vite is running.

1) Confirm the import path mismatch: youâ€™re importing ./components/ui but file is ui.jsx

Vite will resolve ./components/ui if there is a file named:

src/components/ui.js or

src/components/ui.jsx (should work)
â€¦but in your earlier copy step you also had src/components/ui.jsx and at one point you had src/components/ui.jsx exporting different stuff. The real issue is: the file is broken, not the extension.

Still: letâ€™s make it unambiguous by creating src/components/ui/index.js and import that.

2) Create a stable folder module: src/components/ui/index.jsx

Run these commands one at a time (donâ€™t paste huge blocks that you might interrupt):

cd "/Users/jessetorrence/Documents/Work/Coaching 2/AICoachingAppVision/Website Layout/Wireframes by ChatGPT/jt-preview"

rm -rf src/components/ui
mkdir -p src/components/ui


Now create the file using a small paste:

cat > src/components/ui/index.jsx <<'EOF'
import React from "react";

export function cn(...vals) {
  return vals.filter(Boolean).join(" ");
}

export function Badge({ children, className = "" }) {
  return (
    <span className={cn("inline-flex items-center rounded-full border px-2 py-0.5 text-xs font-medium", className)}>
      {children}
    </span>
  );
}

export function Card({ title, children, className = "" }) {
  return (
    <div className={cn("rounded-xl border bg-white p-4 shadow-sm", className)}>
      {title ? <div className="mb-2 text-sm font-semibold">{title}</div> : null}
      {children}
    </div>
  );
}

export function PageHeader({ title, subtitle, right }) {
  return (
    <div className="mb-4 flex items-start justify-between gap-4">
      <div>
        <h1 className="text-xl font-semibold leading-tight">{title}</h1>
        {subtitle ? <p className="mt-1 text-sm opacity-70">{subtitle}</p> : null}
      </div>
      {right ? <div className="shrink-0">{right}</div> : null}
    </div>
  );
}

export function TopBar({ title = "Regenesis" }) {
  return (
    <div className="flex items-center justify-between border-b bg-white px-4 py-3">
      <div className="font-semibold">{title}</div>
      <div className="text-sm opacity-60">Wireframe</div>
    </div>
  );
}

export function LeftRail({ items = [], active, onSelect }) {
  return (
    <div className="w-60 border-r bg-white p-3">
      <div className="mb-2 text-xs font-medium uppercase tracking-wide opacity-60">Navigation</div>
      <div className="flex flex-col gap-2">
        {items.map((it) => (
          <button
            key={it.key}
            onClick={() => onSelect?.(it.key)}
            className={cn(
              "rounded-xl border px-3 py-2 text-left text-sm transition",
              it.key === active ? "bg-gray-100" : "bg-white hover:bg-gray-50"
            )}
          >
            {it.label}
          </button>
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

export function PlaceholderPage({ title = "Coming soon", children }) {
  return (
    <div className="p-6">
      <h2 className="mb-2 text-lg font-semibold">{title}</h2>
      <div className="text-sm opacity-80">{children || "Placeholder content"}</div>
    </div>
  );
}
EOF


Now verify it is valid JS (this is the key sanity check):

node -c src/components/ui/index.jsx


If that prints nothing, it parsed.

3) Update imports to point to the folder module

Your pages import from ../components/ui and your shell imports ./components/ui.

Those will work if src/components/ui/index.jsx exists (Node-style folder resolution).

But Vite sometimes wants explicit extension, so letâ€™s make it explicit and consistent:

Update src/JTCoachingAppShellWireframe.jsx

to:

Fast way (safe, no editor needed):

perl -pi -e 's#from "\./components/ui";#from "./components/ui/index.jsx";#g' src/JTCoachingAppShellWireframe.jsx

Your src/index.css should be ONLY:

@tailwind components;

Why your previous attempts failed (super important)

Every time you saw cat > ... <<'EOF' in your scrollback, your paste got interrupted and you started typing commands before closing EOF. That writes those commands into the file, corrupting it again.

Rule from now on: after you run a cat <<'EOF' command, do not type anything until youâ€™ve pasted the content AND you see the EOF line and your normal prompt returns.

If it still doesnâ€™t render after this

Do exactly this and paste the output:

import React from "react";

/** Utility: minimal className joiner */
export function cn(...vals) {
  return vals.filter(Boolean).join(" ");
}

export function Badge({ children, className = "" }) {
  return (
    <span
      className={cn(
        "inline-flex items-center rounded-full border px-2 py-0.5 text-xs font-medium",
        className
      )}
    >
      {children}
    </span>
  );
}

export function Card({ title, children, className = "" }) {
  return (
    <div className={cn("rounded-xl border bg-white p-4 shadow-sm", className)}>
      {title ? <div className="mb-2 text-sm font-semibold">{title}</div> : null}
      {children}
    </div>
  );
}

export function PageHeader({ title, subtitle, right }) {
  return (
    <div className="mb-4 flex items-start justify-between gap-4">
      <div>
        <h1 className="text-xl font-semibold leading-tight">{title}</h1>
        {subtitle ? <p className="mt-1 text-sm opacity-70">{subtitle}</p> : null}
      </div>
      {right ? <div className="shrink-0">{right}</div> : null}
    </div>
  );
}

/** App shell pieces referenced by JTCoachingAppShellWireframe.jsx */
export function TopBar({ title = "Regenesis" }) {
  return (
    <div className="flex items-center justify-between border-b bg-white px-4 py-3">
      <div className="font-semibold">{title}</div>
      <div className="text-sm opacity-60">Wireframe</div>
    </div>
  );
}

export function LeftRail({ items = [], active, onSelect }) {
  return (
    <div className="w-60 border-r bg-white p-3">
      <div className="mb-2 text-xs font-medium uppercase tracking-wide opacity-60">
        Navigation
      </div>

      <div className="flex flex-col gap-2">
        {items.map((it) => {
          const isActive = it.key === active;
          return (
            <button
              key={it.key}
              onClick={() => onSelect?.(it.key)}
              className={cn(
                "w-full rounded-lg border px-3 py-2 text-left text-sm",
                isActive ? "bg-gray-100" : "bg-white hover:bg-gray-50"
              )}
            >
              <div className="font-medium">{it.label}</div>
              {it.hint ? <div className="text-xs opacity-60">{it.hint}</div> : null}
            </button>
          );
        })}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

export function PlaceholderPage({ title = "Coming soon", children }) {
  return (
    <div className="p-6">
      <h2 className="m-0 mb-2 text-lg font-semibold">{title}</h2>
      <div className="opacity-80">{children || "Placeholder content"}</div>
    </div>
  );
}
EOF

import React from "react";

/** Utility: minimal className joiner */
export function cn(...vals) {
  return vals.filter(Boolean).join(" ");
}

export function Badge({ children, className = "" }) {
  return (
    <span
      className={cn(
        "inline-flex items-center rounded-full border px-2 py-0.5 text-xs font-medium",
        className
      )}
    >
      {children}
    </span>
  );
}

export function Card({ title, children, className = "" }) {
  return (
    <div className={cn("rounded-xl border bg-white p-4 shadow-sm", className)}>
      {title ? <div className="mb-2 text-sm font-semibold">{title}</div> : null}
      {children}
    </div>
  );
}

export function PageHeader({ title, subtitle, right }) {
  return (
    <div className="mb-4 flex items-start justify-between gap-4">
      <div>
        <h1 className="text-xl font-semibold leading-tight">{title}</h1>
        {subtitle ? <p className="mt-1 text-sm opacity-70">{subtitle}</p> : null}
      </div>
      {right ? <div className="shrink-0">{right}</div> : null}
    </div>
  );
}

      <div className="text-sm opacity-60">Wireframe</div>
    </div>
  );
}

export function LeftRail({ items = [], active, onSelect }) {
  return (
    <div className="w-60 border-r bg-white p-3">
      <div className="mb-2 text-xs font-medium uppercase tracking-wide opacity-60">
        Navigation
      </div>

      <div className="flex flex-col gap-2">
        {items.map((it) => {
          const isActive = it.key === active;
          return (
            <button
              key={it.key}
              onClick={() => onSelect?.(it.key)}
              className={cn(
                "w-full rounded-lg border px-3 py-2 text-left text-sm",
                isActive ? "bg-gray-100" : "bg-white hover:bg-gray-50"
              )}
            >
              <div className="font-medium">{it.label}</div>
              {it.hint ? <div className="text-xs opacity-60">{it.hint}</div> : null}
            </button>
          );
        })}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

    </div>

4) The core workflow wiring (best-practice approach)
Google Meet transcript: best current path

Google now has a Google Meet REST API that can access â€œartifactsâ€ like transcripts. Googleâ€™s docs explicitly describe working with artifacts and transcripts, retention windows, and that recordings/transcripts are saved to the organizerâ€™s Drive.

Practical implementation options (choose one now, keep the other as fallback):

Option 1 (recommended): Meet API artifacts (more â€œnativeâ€)

Use Google auth (OAuth) with the correct scopes.

After a meeting ends, find its conference record

List transcripts for that conference record

Fetch transcript entries

Generate draft notes

Notes:

Google states transcripts are saved to the organizerâ€™s Drive and governed by Drive retention rules; transcript entries via the API are deleted after 30 days.

There are also space configs for auto-transcription generation in the Meet API docs, which matters later for â€œalways-onâ€ experiences.

Option 2 (fallback): Drive-based retrieval
Since transcripts live in the organizerâ€™s Drive (Google confirms this), you can also locate the transcript doc via Drive if needed.
This is sometimes easier early, but can be messier to reliably match the right meeting.

My recommendation for your dev this week:

Implement Option 1 if heâ€™s comfortable with Meet API quickly.

If it slows him down, do manual upload of transcript file (drag/drop) for v1 testing, while the Meet API integration is built in parallel.

import { useMemo, useState } from "react";
import "./App.css";
import {
  AppShell,
  SideNav,
  PageHeader,
  Button,
  Card,
  Input,
} from "./components/ui.jsx";

import Dashboard from "./pages/Dashboard.jsx";
import Schedule from "./pages/Schedule.jsx";
import Clients from "./pages/Clients.jsx";
import ResourceLibrary from "./pages/ResourceLibrary.jsx";
import BusinessManagement from "./pages/BusinessManagement.jsx";
import AICompanion from "./pages/AICompanion.jsx";

export default function App() {
  const nav = useMemo(
    () => [
      { key: "dashboard", label: "Dashboard" },
      { key: "clients", label: "Clients" },
      { key: "schedule", label: "Schedule" },
      { key: "library", label: "Resource Library" },
      { key: "business", label: "Business Management" },
      { key: "ai", label: "AI Companion" },
    ],
    []
  );

  const [active, setActive] = useState("dashboard");

  const headerRight = (
    <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
      <Input placeholder="Searchâ€¦" className="w-[260px]" />
      <Button variant="ghost">Settings</Button>
      <Button>New</Button>
    </div>
  );

  return (
    <AppShell
      sidebar={
        <SideNav
          items={nav}
          active={active}
          onSelect={(k) => setActive(k)}
        />
      }
      topbar={<PageHeader title={nav.find((n) => n.key === active)?.label} right={headerRight} />}
    >
      {active === "dashboard" && <Dashboard />}
      {active === "clients" && <Clients />}
      {active === "schedule" && <Schedule />}
      {active === "library" && <ResourceLibrary />}
      {active === "business" && <BusinessManagement />}
      {active === "ai" && <AICompanion />}
    </AppShell>
  );
}

import { useMemo, useState } from "react";
import { Card, Button, Input, Tabs } from "../components/ui.jsx";

const mockClients = [
  { id: "c1", name: "Michael Belles", status: "Active" },
  { id: "c2", name: "Tania Rivera", status: "Active" },
  { id: "c3", name: "Sam Brennan", status: "Active" },
  { id: "c4", name: "Daniel Kim", status: "Paused" },
  { id: "c5", name: "Aisha Patel", status: "Closed" },
  { id: "c6", name: "Jordan Lee", status: "Active" },
  { id: "c7", name: "Priya Nair", status: "Paused" },
  { id: "c8", name: "Omar Haddad", status: "Active" },
  { id: "c9", name: "Elena Garcia", status: "Active" },
  { id: "c10", name: "Noah Stein", status: "Active" },
];

export default function Clients() {
  const [selectedId, setSelectedId] = useState("c1");
  const [filter, setFilter] = useState("Active"); // Active | All | Paused | Closed
  const [q, setQ] = useState("");
  const [tab, setTab] = useState("Overview");

  const selected = mockClients.find((c) => c.id === selectedId) || mockClients[0];

  const list = useMemo(() => {
    return mockClients
      .filter((c) => (filter === "All" ? true : c.status === filter))
      .filter((c) => c.name.toLowerCase().includes(q.toLowerCase()));
  }, [filter, q]);

  return (
    <div className="h-[calc(100vh-88px)]">
      <div className="grid h-full grid-cols-[320px_1fr] gap-4">
        {/* LEFT: client list stays visible */}
        <Card className="h-full overflow-hidden p-0">
          <div className="border-b p-3">
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
              <div className="text-sm font-semibold">Clients</div>
              <div className="flex gap-1">
                <Button size="sm" variant={filter === "Active" ? "default" : "ghost"} onClick={() => setFilter("Active")}>
                  Active
                </Button>
                <Button size="sm" variant={filter === "All" ? "default" : "ghost"} onClick={() => setFilter("All")}>
                  View all
                </Button>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div className="mt-2">
              <Input value={q} onChange={(e) => setQ(e.target.value)} placeholder="Search clientsâ€¦" />
            </div>
            <div className="mt-2 flex gap-2">
              <Button size="sm" variant={filter === "Paused" ? "default" : "ghost"} onClick={() => setFilter("Paused")}>
                Paused
              </Button>
              <Button size="sm" variant={filter === "Closed" ? "default" : "ghost"} onClick={() => setFilter("Closed")}>
                Closed
              </Button>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div className="h-full overflow-auto p-2">
            {list.map((c) => {
              const active = c.id === selectedId;
              return (
                <button
                  key={c.id}
                  onClick={() => setSelectedId(c.id)}
                  className={[
                    "w-full rounded-xl border p-3 text-left transition",
                    active ? "bg-black text-white" : "bg-white hover:bg-zinc-50",
                  ].join(" ")}
                >
                  <div className="font-medium">{c.name}</div>
                  <div className={["text-xs opacity-70", active ? "text-white/70" : ""].join(" ")}>
                    {c.status}
                  </div>
                </button>
              );
            })}
            {list.length === 0 ? (
              <div className="p-4 text-sm opacity-60">No clients match your filters.</div>
            ) : null}
          </div>
        </Card>

        {/* RIGHT: selected client workspace */}
        <div className="flex h-full flex-col gap-4">
          <Card className="p-4">
            <div className="flex items-start justify-between">
              <div>
                <div className="text-lg font-semibold leading-tight">{selected.name}</div>
                <div className="text-sm opacity-70">Client workspace</div>
              </div>
              <div className="flex gap-2">
                <Button variant="ghost">Message</Button>
                <Button>New session note</Button>
              </div>
            </div>

            <div className="mt-4">
              <Tabs
                value={tab}
                onChange={setTab}
                items={[
                  "Overview",
                  "Session Notes",
                  "T-15 Prep",
                  "Progress",
                  "Client Resources",
                  "Admin",
                ]}
              />
            </div>
          </Card>

          <div className="grid grid-cols-12 gap-4">
            <Card className="col-span-7" title={tab}>
              <div className="text-sm opacity-80">
                {tab === "Overview" && "High-level snapshot of goals, themes, commitments, and recent activity."}
                {tab === "Session Notes" && "Draft/edit/send post-session notes. (Core v1 functionality lives here.)"}
                {tab === "T-15 Prep" && "Pre-session prep checklist + prompts + prior commitments."}
                {tab === "Progress" && "Goals, milestones, trends, and qualitative changes over time."}
                {tab === "Client Resources" && "Only resources youâ€™ve shared with this client."}
                {tab === "Admin" && "Client-specific agreements, waivers, billing status, and logistics."}
              </div>

              <div className="mt-4 rounded-xl border bg-zinc-50 p-4 text-sm">
                Mock content area (weâ€™ll replace with your real layouts tomorrow/next).
              </div>
            </Card>

            <Card className="col-span-5" title="Right rail">
              <div className="text-sm opacity-80">
                Action panel: next session, commitments, nudges, reminders, AI highlights.
              </div>
              <div className="mt-4 space-y-2">
                <div className="rounded-xl border p-3 text-sm">Next session: Thu 3:00 PM</div>
                <div className="rounded-xl border p-3 text-sm">Last commitment: â€œHave the hard convoâ€</div>
                <div className="rounded-xl border p-3 text-sm">AI insight: â€œAvoidance pattern presentâ€</div>
              </div>
            </Card>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
